He is therefore removed to His private apartment, where no one can see Him. Actually, during this period renovations are made on the body of the JagannÄtha Deity. This is called nava-yauvana. During the Ratha-yÄtrÄ ceremony, Lord JagannÄtha once again comes before the public. Thus for fifteen days after the bathing ceremony, Lord JagannÄtha is not visible to any visitors.

patraá¹ puá¹£paá¹ phalaá¹ toyaá¹ yo me bhaktyÄ prayacchati

Pure devotion is uncontaminated by the modes of material nature. Ahaituky apratihatÄ: unconditional devotional service cannot be checked by any material condition. This means that one does not have to be very rich to serve the Supreme Personality of Godhead. Even the poorest man can equally serve the Supreme Personality of Godhead if he has pure devotion. If there is no ulterior motive, devotional service cannot be checked by any material condition.
